//GAME NAME:		Telefang 2 - Power (GBA)

// Define a TABLE
#VAR(Table, TABLE)
#VAR(engTableOld, TABLE)
#VAR(engTable, TABLE)

// Load and activate the table
#ADDTBL("script/telefang.tbl", Table)
#ADDTBL("script/dos-dialogue.tbl", engTableOld)
#ADDTBL("script/translation.tbl", engTable)
